unk unk will still serve as acting head of state during the king 's frequent unk from the country . </s> <s> `` the major political crisis in the country has been resolved and the political deadlock facing the nation has also come to an end , '' the king said in his statement . </s> <s> the senate will initially be appointed by the king . </s> <s> the agreement did not say how many seats there would be , nor how they would be divided . </s> <s> the parties will hammer out details later . </s> <s> unk than , one of ranariddh 's negotiators , said the senate would serve a mostly advisory role to the assembly . </s> <s> the senior senate leaders will join those of the assembly , the prime minister and the country 's top two unk unk in a delicate balance of power on the council that will of a government between the cpp and ranariddh 's unk funcinpec to allow international donors and businesses to again operate in the unk country , which is in desperate need of aid . </s> <s> it could <d> <p> <s> cambodian politicians expressed hope monday that a new partnership between the parties of strongman hun sen and his rival , prince norodom ranariddh , in a coalition government would not end in more violence . </s> <s> hun sen and ranariddh , co-prime ministers in a coalition formed in 1993 after a unk u.n.-sponsored election , often clashed over unk and the integration of guerrilla fighters from the unk khmer rouge . </s> <s> their arguments turned bloody last year when hun sen ousted ranariddh in a coup . </s> <s> the prince fled cambodia and did not return until a few months before elections in july . </s> <s> hun sen 's cambodian people 's party narrowly won the polls , but a strong unk finish by ranariddh 's funcinpec gave the unk party leverage in unk negotiations . </s> <s> after a three-month unk , they agreed last week to a coalition deal that will make hun sen sole prime minister and ranariddh president of the national assembly . </s> <s> `` this will not be a unk of 1993 because there will not be two prime ministers , '' said hun sen aide prak unk , who attended last week 's summit . </s> <s> `` when we had two prime ministers , everything moved very slowly and decisions were made more politically than technically . '' </s> <s> ranariddh said saturday that the two parties agreed to keep the ministries of interior and defense under unk . </s> <s> senior funcinpec official ahmad unk revealed monday that it was also agreed that the cpp would control the foreign affairs and finance unk . </s> <s> funcinpec will take justice and information . </s> <s> the parties are to form working groups this week to divide remaining government posts and draft a constitutional amendment to form a new senate . </s> <s> hun sen and ranariddh are scheduled to meet nov. 23 _ two days before parliament unk _ to review the results of the working groups and give their final approval , ahmad unk said . </s> <s> their ability to repair their relationship and work together will be the key to a stable coalition . </s> <s> `` i consider this a unk , '' ahmad unk said . </s> <s> `` they have to be careful with the way they work and what they say . </s> <s> they will have to compromise to achieve results . '' </s> <s> ranariddh 's ally , sam rainsy , whose party placed a distant third in the election , was left out of last week 's deal . </s> <s> sam rainsy , a unk critic of hun sen , and his party 's 14 other members of parliament have remained outside cambodia since september amid fears for their security . </s> <s> in a letter to king norodom sihanouk released monday , sam rainsy complained that hun sen had not responded to his unk on security , making it unk for his people to return for the unk of parliament . </s> <s> sam rainsy said he had been told by ranariddh that his party and former khmer rouge guerrillas had been implicated by hun sen in a rocket attack on the sept. 24 opening of parliament . </s> <s> authorities have called it an assassination attempt on hun sen. a police general investigating the attack said monday that likely suspects have been identified , but he would not reveal names or their political unk . </s> </p> </d> # <d> hun sen , prince ranariddh share power in new coalition cambodian government </d>

'' </s> <s> ranariddh 's ally , sam rainsy , whose party placed a distant third in the election , was left out of last week 's deal . </s> <s> sam rainsy , a unk critic of hun sen , and his party 's 14 other members of parliament have remained outside cambodia since september amid fears for their security . </s> <s> in a letter to king norodom sihanouk released monday , sam rainsy complained that hun sen had not responded to his unk on security , making it unk for his people to return for the unk of parliament . </s> <s> sam rainsy said he had been told by ranariddh that his party and former khmer rouge guerrillas had been implicated by hun sen in a rocket attack on the sept. 24 opening of parliament . </s> <s> authorities have called it an assassination attempt on hun sen. a police general investigating the attack said monday that likely suspects have been identified , but he would not reveal names or their political unk . </s> </p> </d> # <d> cambodian coalition formed between hun sen and ranariddh . rainsy left out . </d>

</s> <s> after unk several hundred kilometers ( miles ) through unk tropical forest , thousands of rebel fighters have gathered 19 kilometers ( 11 miles ) outside kindu , where troops loyal to remove the last government stronghold in eastern congo and unk the way for rebel advance into the unk southwest . </s> <s> a rebel defeat , on the other hand , would put the coalition of ethnic tutsis , disenchanted members of the congolese army and opposition politicians on the unk and give a boost to kabila 's efforts to unk off the rebellion launched aug. 2 . </s> <s> rebel commander richard meeting stiff resistance in the town , he said . </s> <s> since the assault on the town began at 3 a.m. ( unk gmt ) , at least 18 enemy soldiers were killed and 40 taken prisoner , mondo said , adding the number was expected to rise . </s> <s> the rebels took casualties , too , but the number was not known . </s> <s> one rebel soldier was wounded in the stomach , he said . </s> <s> he said the large kindu air base , 4 kilometers ( 2 miles ) outside town , was unk and no one appeared to be in control . </s> <s> `` our soldiers are in the town and the fighting is continuing , '' rebel unk before the cut , now 3 percent . </s> <s> however , interest rate levels had become a contentious political issue with center-left governments in germany and france pushing for rate cuts to help spur '' </s> <s> if the crisis comes to a confidence vote and prodi loses , he would offer his resignation . </s> <s> once he does that , it is up to scalfaro to decide what to do . </s> <s> he could ask prodi or someone else to form a new government or he could call elections 2 1/2 years early , something most analysts think unlikely . </s> <s> working in prodi 's favor is the fact that few parties think they would stand to gain by early elections , including the communist unk . </s> <s> there was speculation prodi would reopen negotiations that would win back the communists ' unk support , as he has managed to do in the past . </s> <s> prodi 's government has held together this long in large part because of the widely shared desire to see italy qualify for participation in the 1999 debut of europe 's common currency , the euro . </s> <s> that happened earlier this year _ leaving the unk allies without so clear a reason to stay together . </s> <s> prodi leads italy 's unk government since world war ii . </s> <s> he has unk all but unk unk , who served 3 { years in two back-to-back unk from 1983 to 1987 . </s> <s> unk is not part of prodi 's center-left coalition , but the government needs its 34 votes to unk a majority in the lower house . </s> <s> it has been a difficult ally from the outset . </s> <s> it broke with prodi over nato expansion earlier this year and on sending troops into albania last year . </s> <s> prodi was even forced to resign a year ago after a bitter battle over spending cuts linked to the euro . </s> <s> the crisis was resolved , and prodi returned to work , after he made steep concessions and promised a unk work week . </s> </p> </d> # <d> cutting deficit key to italy 's euro use . unk unk as party president . </d>
